Ambiance: 4 (chill)
Service: 4 (Thanks)
Cleanliness: 5 (shining)

Overall: ‚ú¶‚ú¶‚ú¶.8

This sushi restaurant is definitely a hidden gem in Venice; people should at least give it a try once. Ambience is on point and perfect for a cute little date with your friends or significant other. In terms of tasting, I thought their sushi was just okay but I do highly recommend their crispy rice. Its crunchiness and savoriness definitely hit my spot. Otherwise, the presentation of dishes is work of art. Price is reasonable ($30-$50 per person).

It's a good starter for fancy sushi restaurant.<//review><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPFhcC4dTsi6_fm7e2fzBSaYicDQmLFJsHoF9nS=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pics>< resp>

< date>

<Text>I am obsessed! Okay so I was driving around Venice and saw this restaurant from my car and immediately had to look up what it was/what it was called because it looked like a magical fairy garden. The vibes are on point!!! Seriously whoever designed this place knows what they are doing. I made a reservation to come with my boyfriend on a Thursday (during covid times). Luckily we made a reservation because there was over an hour wait for people who were doing standby. Our table was ready when we arrived and we were seated immediately. Again, the vibes were SO fun! Closest thing I have gotten to the club in a while. The bar is inside and they were bumping music similar to other sushi restaurants in LA. All of the waiters were wearing both masks and shields and were very attentive.

First, the drinks. Okay, if you are coming here you MUST try their drinks. They are so intricate, unique, beautiful, and DELICIOUS.
- Lychee on Rose Cocktail: Grey Goose, lemon, pomegranate, lychee, elderflower, citrus. This was 1 beautiful and 2 soo tasty. It was light, but also so flavorful.
- She So Sour: Japanese whiskey, lemon, lime, honey, passionfruit, egg whites, 24K gold!!! Like what?? Gold flakes on top!!! This was amazing. Definitely will be getting this the next time we come back.
- Yuzu O'Fashioned: delicious, classic old fashioned with Troy Boy's secret recipe.
- The Upper West Side: very good also!
- Sake: Snow Maiden Nigori

Second, the food. Ughhh such amazing food. Sushi is my favorite and this place definitely made the cut. This is what we ordered:
- Chili garlic edamame: edamame is always a must! The chili garlic flavor added a delicious kick.
- Crispy Rice: my absolute favorite meal. This was prepared perfectly and in the perfect portion size.
- Foxxy roll: This was recommended to use by the waiter and it was so incredible. It was a combination of several different fish, so it was also very filling.
- Shrimp Tempura roll: classic and flavorful. I can never go wrong with a shrimp tempura roll. Pair with wasabi and it's delicious.
- Tiger King is the absolute best roll on the menu! You must try. I have ordered it several times and each time it's amazing.
- Rick James is my second favorite. I highly recommend trying it if you like halibut, spicy tuna and yellowtail.
- I don't recommend the Baked Crab Roll. It is very bland and disappointing.

Dessert:
- Orange Ricotta Doughnut Holes: the donuts were very good and satisfying. Although, the dips (strawberry & apple) weren't very good.

I cannot wait to be back for more amazing vibes, drinks, and food :)</Text>< username>

< Text>
Upon exiting the Lyft you're greeted to a lovely, vibrant street scene that is colorful and lively. Once you enter, the bar wraps around one side of the room with unique individuals sipping what seems to be concoctions out of a speakeasy.  I was almost tempted to have a seat but the hostess, with the mostest (sp), Ms. Kim, greets me with a smile as wide and bright as Chester da Cheetah and asks "If I'd be dining or drinking tonight?" My reply, "both", "Well I have the perfect table for you."

I started with a seaweed salad and a Green Tea-Wi. The Japanese whiskey in the Tea-Wi was flavorful, full bodied and just delicious. The seaweed had just the right amount of crunch to compliment the drink, since I'd chosen the drink first.

My dinner was a Sashimi Plate. An assortment of perfectly apportioned slices of fresh fish that dissolves in your mouth quickly, but slow enough for the taste to linger...Salmon....Red Snapper....Tuna...Yellow Tail, aww the YT was supreme and Halibut was glorious.  All were delicious and tasted like they were just cut off the whole fish in the back.

Brent, the restaurant manager, learned that I had just arrived for a meeting at 2pm and that I'd be departing at 5am. So he wanted to do something special since I'd chosen his establishment for my first and last meal of the day.  He ordered a Signature Dish called "The Ava".  Heaven help me find room in my stomach to eat all 6 pieces of this seared salmon, ponzu, micro greens, Farmer's Market Fruit, Serrano, truffle oil and a little Magic dish. Ever have a blueberry dipped in truffle oil? Neither have I! But the raspberry dipped was fabulous. Especially with the seared salmon! I'm done, stick a fork in me!

My server, Lindsay, kept the drinks flowing...flowing.... did I say Flowing?! The Smoke & Salt was the liquid dessert that made me feel like I was floating in air. Well done Wabi Sabi, well done<//Text>

<date>1477945743599</date><Rate>4<//Rate>< Review>
Went to Wabi-Sabi for a little pre-birthday-cocktail dinner with the SO. It had a large alcoholic bar section up front with a sushi bar tucked away at the rear. We found seating in the sushi bar.
First impression: a little too lush and distracting for a good sushi bar. Second and final impression: first impressions don't matter. The food was balanced, tasteful and well presented. The drinks were stiff-ish. The wasabi was real. Apart from the decor, nothing in the place puts you off balance. You should get some food here if you can. I'll want to go again if I'm in the neighborhood< /Review>

< Review>
An excellent resource if you need boxes - moving, run an eBay store, relocating a large amount of inventory, taking apart a Harley Davidson motorcycle then taking it to a person who knows how to put it back together because it didn't look that hard on Youtube..

The spot has a relaxed, no pressure staff who are knowledgable and friendly. The Zoners really seem to enjoy their jobs. Says something about the management right there.

The prices are way lower than Staples, Office Depot or The Home Depot on boxes. I don't know about their prices on shipping.

Oh yeah, they also ship things. All sorts of things. I went in once and the guy was shipping a stuffed swordfish! Another time, a car bumper. I wouldn't know where to begin to ship things like that. Well, I suppose it is a good thing I don't work here, then.</Review>
